        public Ventoy()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
            DataContext = this;

            _ = RefreshUsbListAsync();
        }

        private void OnPropertyChanged(string name) =>
            PropertyChanged?.Invoke(this, new PropertyChangedEventArgs(name));

        private async void UpdateDeviceInfo()
        {
            if (SelectedDrive == null)
            {
                DeviceInfoText = "РЈСҒСӮСҖРҫР№СҒСӮРІРҫ РҪРө РІСӢРұСҖР°РҪРҫ.";
                return;
            }

            try
            {
                var di = SelectedDrive.ToDriveInfo();
                if (di == null || !di.IsReady)
                {
                    DeviceInfoText = $"{SelectedDrive.DisplayName}\nР”РёСҒРә РҪРө РіРҫСӮРҫРІ.";
                    return;
                }

                long total = di.TotalSize;
                long free = di.TotalFreeSpace;
                long used = total - free;
                double usedPercent = total > 0 ? Math.Round(used * 100.0 / total, 1) : 0.0;

                SelectedDrive.TotalBytes = total;
                SelectedDrive.FreeBytes = free;
                SelectedDrive.UsedPercent = usedPercent;

                DeviceInfoText = $"{SelectedDrive.DisplayName}\nРңРөСӮРәР°: {di.VolumeLabel}\nР’СҒРөРіРҫ: {FormatBytes(total)} вҖў РЎРІРҫРұРҫРҙРҪРҫ: {FormatBytes(free)} вҖў Р—Р°РҪСҸСӮРҫ: {usedPercent}%";
            }
            catch
            {
                DeviceInfoText = $"{SelectedDrive.DisplayName}\nРһСҲРёРұРәР° СҮСӮРөРҪРёСҸ. Р’РҫР·РјРҫР¶РҪРҫ, СғСҒСӮСҖРҫР№СҒСӮРІРҫ РҪРө РіРҫСӮРҫРІРҫ РёР»Рё РҝРҫРІСҖРөР¶РҙРөРҪРҫ.";
            }

            OnPropertyChanged(nameof(SelectedDrive));
            await ScanIsoImagesAsync();
        }

        private async Task ScanIsoImagesAsync()
        {
            // РһСҮРёСүР°РөРј СҒРҝРёСҒРҫРә РІ РҝРҫСӮРҫРәРө UI
            await Dispatcher.InvokeAsync(FoundIsoImages.Clear);

            if (SelectedDrive == null) return;
            var driveInfo = SelectedDrive.ToDriveInfo();
            if (driveInfo == null || !driveInfo.IsReady) return;

            // РҹСҖРҫРІРөСҖРәР°, СҮСӮРҫ Ventoy СғСҒСӮР°РҪРҫРІР»РөРҪ
            if (!IsVentoyInstalled(SelectedDrive)) return;

            try
            {
                var images = await Task.Run(() =>
                {
                    var foundFiles = new List<IsoImageItem>();
                    var extensions = new[] { "*.iso", "*.img" };

                    // --- РҳР—РңР•РқР•РқРҳР•: РҹРҫР»СғСҮР°РөРј РҝСғСӮСҢ Рә РҝР°РҝРәРө ISO ---
                    string rootPath = driveInfo.RootDirectory.FullName;
                    string isoFolderPath = Path.Combine(rootPath, "ISO");
                    var isoDir = new DirectoryInfo(isoFolderPath);

                    // Р•СҒР»Рё РҝР°РҝРәРё ISO РҪРөСӮ, РҝСҖРҫСҒСӮРҫ РІРҫР·РІСҖР°СүР°РөРј РҝСғСҒСӮРҫР№ СҒРҝРёСҒРҫРә (РёР»Рё РјРҫР¶РҪРҫ РёСҒРәР°СӮСҢ РІ РәРҫСҖРҪРө РәР°Рә Р·Р°РҝР°СҒРҪРҫР№ РІР°СҖРёР°РҪСӮ)
                    if (!isoDir.Exists)
                    {
                        return foundFiles;
                    }

                    foreach (var ext in extensions)
                    {
                        // РҳСүРөРј С„Р°Р№Р»СӢ РІРҪСғСӮСҖРё РҝР°РҝРәРё G:\ISO\
                        // SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly РұРөСҖРөСӮ С„Р°Р№Р»СӢ СӮРҫР»СҢРәРҫ РёР· РҝР°РҝРәРё ISO (РұРөР· РІР»РҫР¶РөРҪРҪСӢС…)
                        foreach (var file in isoDir.GetFiles(ext, SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly))
                        {
                            foundFiles.Add(new IsoImageItem
                            {
                                FileName = file.Name,
                                FullPath = file.FullName,
                                Size = FormatBytes(file.Length)
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    return foundFiles.OrderBy(f => f.FileName).ToList();
                });

                // РһРұРҪРҫРІР»СҸРөРј РәРҫР»Р»РөРәСҶРёСҺ РІ РҝРҫСӮРҫРәРө UI
                await Dispatcher.InvokeAsync(() =>
                {
                    foreach (var item in images)
                    {
                        FoundIsoImages.Add(item);
                    }
                });
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Debug.WriteLine($"РһСҲРёРұРәР° СҒРәР°РҪРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёСҸ ISO: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        private static string FormatBytes(long bytes)
        {
            const long KB = 1024;
            const long MB = KB * 1024;
            const long GB = MB * 1024;
            if (bytes >= GB) return $"{Math.Round(bytes / (double)GB, 2)} GB";
            if (bytes >= MB) return $"{Math.Round(bytes / (double)MB, 2)} MB";
            if (bytes >= KB) return $"{Math.Round(bytes / (double)KB, 2)} KB";
            return $"{bytes} B";
        }

        private async void RefreshButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            await RefreshUsbListAsync();
        }

        private async Task RefreshUsbListAsync()
        {
            try
            {
                IsRefreshing = true;
                await Task.Delay(350);

                var drives = DriveInfo.GetDrives()
                    .Where(d => d.DriveType == DriveType.Removable && d.IsReady)
                    .ToArray();

                await Dispatcher.InvokeAsync(() =>
                {
                    UsbDrives.Clear();
                    foreach (var d in drives)
                    {
                        try
                        {
                            var item = new UsbDriveItem
                            {
                                DriveLetter = d.RootDirectory.FullName.Replace("\\", ""),
                                VolumeLabel = SafeGet(() => d.VolumeLabel, string.Empty),
                                DisplayName = $"{d.Name} {(string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(d.VolumeLabel) ? "" : $"{d.VolumeLabel}")}",
                                TotalBytes = SafeGet(() => d.TotalSize, 0L),
                                FreeBytes = SafeGet(() => d.TotalFreeSpace, 0L)
                            };
                            item.UsedPercent = item.TotalBytes > 0
                                ? Math.Round((item.TotalBytes - item.FreeBytes) * 100.0 / item.TotalBytes, 1)
                                : 0.0;
                            UsbDrives.Add(item);
                        }
                        catch { continue; }
                    }

                    if (UsbDrives.Count == 0)
                    {
                        DeviceInfoText = "РЎСҠС‘РјРҪСӢРө USB-СғСҒСӮСҖРҫР№СҒСӮРІР° РҪРө РҪР°Р№РҙРөРҪСӢ.";
                        SelectedDrive = null;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        if (SelectedDrive != null)
                        {
                            var found = UsbDrives.FirstOrDefault(x => x.DriveLetter == SelectedDrive.DriveLetter);
                            if (found != null) SelectedDrive = found;
                        }
                        if (SelectedDrive == null && UsbDrives.Count > 0) SelectedDrive = UsbDrives[0];
                    }
                }, DispatcherPriority.Background);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show($"РһСҲРёРұРәР° РҝСҖРё СҒРәР°РҪРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёРё USB: {ex.Message}", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.OK);
            }
            finally
            {
                IsRefreshing = false;
            }
        }

        private static T SafeGet<T>(Func<T> getter, T fallback)
        {
            try { return getter(); }
            catch { return fallback; }
        }

        // ------------------- РӨРҫСҖРјР°СӮРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёРө СҮРөСҖРөР· DiskPart -------------------
        private async void FormatButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (SelectedDrive == null)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show("Р’СӢРұРөСҖРёСӮРө РҪР°РәРҫРҝРёСӮРөР»СҢ РҙР»СҸ С„РҫСҖРјР°СӮРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёСҸ.", "Р’РҪРёРјР°РҪРёРө", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.OK);
                return;
            }

            var res = CustomMessageBox.Show($"Р’СӢ РҙРөР№СҒСӮРІРёСӮРөР»СҢРҪРҫ С…РҫСӮРёСӮРө С„РҫСҖРјР°СӮРёСҖРҫРІР°СӮСҢ {SelectedDrive.DisplayName}?\nР’СҒРө РҙР°РҪРҪСӢРө РҪР° СғСҒСӮСҖРҫР№СҒСӮРІРө РұСғРҙСғСӮ СғРҙР°Р»РөРҪСӢ.", "РҹРҫРҙСӮРІРөСҖРҙРёСӮРө С„РҫСҖРјР°СӮРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёРө", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.YesNo);
            if (res != CustomMessageBox.MessageBoxResult.Yes) return;

            try
            {
                IsRefreshing = true;
                DeviceInfoText = "РӨРҫСҖРјР°СӮРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёРө... РҹРҫРҙРҫР¶РҙРёСӮРө.";

                await Task.Run(() =>
                {
                    // РһРҝСҖРөРҙРөР»СҸРөРј РҙРёСҒРә РҝРҫ РҪРҫРјРөСҖСғ С„РёР·РёСҮРөСҒРәРҫРіРҫ РҙРёСҒРәР°
                    var drive = SelectedDrive.ToDriveInfo();
                    if (drive == null)
                        throw new Exception("РқРө СғРҙР°Р»РҫСҒСҢ РҝРҫР»СғСҮРёСӮСҢ РёРҪС„РҫСҖРјР°СҶРёСҺ Рҫ РҙРёСҒРәРө.");

                    string diskNumber = GetDiskNumber(drive.RootDirectory.FullName);
                    if (diskNumber == null)
                        throw new Exception("РқРө СғРҙР°Р»РҫСҒСҢ РҫРҝСҖРөРҙРөР»РёСӮСҢ РҪРҫРјРөСҖ С„РёР·РёСҮРөСҒРәРҫРіРҫ РҙРёСҒРәР° РҙР»СҸ DiskPart.");

                    // РЎРҫР·РҙР°С‘Рј РІСҖРөРјРөРҪРҪСӢР№ СҒРәСҖРёРҝСӮ DiskPart
                    string scriptPath = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), "diskpart_script.txt");
                    File.WriteAllText(scriptPath,
$@"select disk {diskNumber}
clean
create partition primary
format fs=FAT32 quick
assign
exit");

                    // Р—Р°РҝСғСҒРә DiskPart
                    ProcessStartInfo psi = new ProcessStartInfo
                    {
                        FileName = "diskpart.exe",
                        Arguments = $"/s \"{scriptPath}\"",
                        UseShellExecute = false,
                        CreateNoWindow = true,
                        RedirectStandardOutput = true,
                        RedirectStandardError = true
                    };

                    using var proc = Process.Start(psi);
                    proc?.WaitForExit();
                    int exitCode = proc?.ExitCode ?? 1;
                    if (exitCode != 0)
                        throw new Exception($"DiskPart Р·Р°РІРөСҖСҲРёР»СҒСҸ СҒ РәРҫРҙРҫРј {exitCode}.");
                });

                CustomMessageBox.Show("РӨРҫСҖРјР°СӮРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёРө Р·Р°РІРөСҖСҲРөРҪРҫ.", "Р“РҫСӮРҫРІРҫ", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.OK);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show($"РһСҲРёРұРәР° С„РҫСҖРјР°СӮРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёСҸ: {ex.Message}", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.OK);
            }
            finally
            {
                IsRefreshing = false;
                await RefreshUsbListAsync();
                await ScanIsoImagesAsync();
            }
        }

        private string? GetDiskNumber(string driveLetter)
        {
            // РҹРҫР»СғСҮР°РөРј С„РёР·РёСҮРөСҒРәРёР№ РҙРёСҒРә СҮРөСҖРөР· WMI
            try
            {
                var query = $"ASSOCIATORS OF {{Win32_LogicalDisk.DeviceID='{driveLetter.TrimEnd('\\')}'}} WHERE AssocClass=Win32_LogicalDiskToPartition";
                var searcher = new System.Management.ManagementObjectSearcher(query);
                foreach (System.Management.ManagementObject partition in searcher.Get())
                {
                    string deviceId = partition["DeviceID"]?.ToString(); // РҪР°РҝСҖРёРјРөСҖ "Disk #1, Partition #0"
                    if (deviceId != null && deviceId.Contains("#"))
                    {
                        int idx = deviceId.IndexOf('#') + 1;
                        int comma = deviceId.IndexOf(',', idx);
                        string num = comma > 0 ? deviceId.Substring(idx, comma - idx) : deviceId.Substring(idx);
                        return num.Trim();
                    }
                }
            }
            catch { }
            return null;
        }

        // ------------------- Ventoy СғСҒСӮР°РҪРҫРІРәР°/РҫРұРҪРҫРІР»РөРҪРёРө -------------------
        private async void InstallButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => await RunVentoyAsync(true);
        private async void UpdateButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => await RunVentoyAsync(false);

        private async Task RunVentoyAsync(bool install)
        {
            if (SelectedDrive == null)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show("Р’СӢРұРөСҖРёСӮРө РҪР°РәРҫРҝРёСӮРөР»СҢ РҙР»СҸ РҫРҝРөСҖР°СҶРёРё.", "Р’РҪРёРјР°РҪРёРө", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.OK);
                return;
            }

            try
            {
                IsRefreshing = true;
                DeviceInfoText = install ? "РЈСҒСӮР°РҪРҫРІРәР° Ventoy... РҹРҫРҙРҫР¶РҙРёСӮРө." : "РһРұРҪРҫРІР»РөРҪРёРө Ventoy... РҹРҫРҙРҫР¶РҙРёСӮРө.";

                await Task.Run(() =>
                {
                    string ventoyPath = Path.Combine(AppDomain.CurrentDomain.BaseDirectory, "Ventoy", "Ventoy2Disk.exe");
                    if (!File.Exists(ventoyPath))
                        throw new FileNotFoundException("РқРө РҪР°Р№РҙРөРҪ Ventoy2Disk.exe РІ РҝР°РҝРәРө Ventoy.", ventoyPath);

                    string driveParam = $"/Drive:{SelectedDrive.DriveLetter}";
                    string modeParam = install ? "/I" : "/U";

                    ProcessStartInfo psi = new ProcessStartInfo
                    {
                        FileName = ventoyPath,
                        Arguments = $"VTOYCLI {modeParam} {driveParam}",
                        CreateNoWindow = true,
                        UseShellExecute = false,
                        RedirectStandardOutput = true,
                        RedirectStandardError = true
                    };

                    using var proc = Process.Start(psi);
                    proc?.WaitForExit();
                    int exitCode = proc?.ExitCode ?? 1;
                    if (exitCode != 0)
                        throw new Exception($"Ventoy Р·Р°РІРөСҖСҲРёР»СҒСҸ СҒ РәРҫРҙРҫРј {exitCode}.");
                });

                CustomMessageBox.Show(install ? "РЈСҒСӮР°РҪРҫРІРәР° Ventoy Р·Р°РІРөСҖСҲРөРҪР°." : "РһРұРҪРҫРІР»РөРҪРёРө Ventoy Р·Р°РІРөСҖСҲРөРҪРҫ.", "Р“РҫСӮРҫРІРҫ", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.OK);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show($"РһСҲРёРұРәР° РҝСҖРё Р·Р°РҝСғСҒРәРө Ventoy: {ex.Message}", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.OK);
            }
            finally
            {
                IsRefreshing = false;
                await RefreshUsbListAsync();
            }
        }

        private void IsoBox_SelectionChanged(object sender, SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (Browse != null && LocalFilePathTextBox != null) { 
                if (IsoBox.SelectedIndex == 0)
                {
                    Browse.IsEnabled = true;
                    LocalFilePathTextBox.IsEnabled = true;
                }
                else
                {
                    Browse.IsEnabled = false;
                    LocalFilePathTextBox.IsEnabled = false;
                }
                if (IsoBox.SelectedItem is ComboBoxItem selectedItem)
                {
                    // 2. РҹРҫР»СғСҮР°РөРј СҒРІРҫР№СҒСӮРІРҫ Tag. РһРҪРҫ РёРјРөРөСӮ СӮРёРҝ object.
                    object tagValue = selectedItem.Tag;

                    // 3. РҹСҖРҫРІРөСҖСҸРөРј, СҮСӮРҫ Tag РҪРө null, Рё РҝСҖРёРІРҫРҙРёРј РөРіРҫ Рә СҒСӮСҖРҫРәРө
                    if (tagValue != null)
                    {
                        // Р’РҫР·РІСҖР°СүР°РөРј Р·РҪР°СҮРөРҪРёРө Tag, РҝСҖРөРҫРұСҖР°Р·РҫРІР°РҪРҪРҫРө РІ СҒСӮСҖРҫРәСғ
                        LocalFilePathTextBox.Text = tagValue.ToString();
                    }
                    else { LocalFilePathTextBox.Text = ""; }
                }
            }

        }

        private void BrowseButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            // 1. РЎРҫР·РҙР°РөРј РҫРұСҠРөРәСӮ OpenFileDialog
            OpenFileDialog openFileDialog = new OpenFileDialog();

            // 2. РқР°СҒСӮСҖР°РёРІР°РөРј С„РёР»СҢСӮСҖ РҙР»СҸ .iso С„Р°Р№Р»РҫРІ
            // Format: "РўРөРәСҒСӮРҫРІРҫРө РҫРҝРёСҒР°РҪРёРө | *.СҖР°СҒСҲРёСҖРөРҪРёРө"
            // Р”РҫРұР°РІР»СҸРөРј РҫРҝСҶРёСҺ "Р’СҒРө С„Р°Р№Р»СӢ (*.*)" РҙР»СҸ СғРҙРҫРұСҒСӮРІР°
            openFileDialog.Filter = "РһРұСҖР°Р·СӢ ISO (*.iso)|*.iso|Р’СҒРө С„Р°Р№Р»СӢ (*.*)|*.*";

            // 3. РЈСҒСӮР°РҪР°РІР»РёРІР°РөРј Р·Р°РіРҫР»РҫРІРҫРә РҫРәРҪР°
            openFileDialog.Title = "Р’СӢРұРөСҖРёСӮРө ISO-С„Р°Р№Р»";

            // 4. РһСӮРәСҖСӢРІР°РөРј РҙРёР°Р»РҫРіРҫРІРҫРө РҫРәРҪРҫ. ShowDialog() РІРҫР·РІСҖР°СүР°РөСӮ bool?
            bool? result = openFileDialog.ShowDialog();

            // 5. РһРұСҖР°РұР°СӮСӢРІР°РөРј СҖРөР·СғР»СҢСӮР°СӮ
            if (result == true)
            {
                // РҹРҫР»СҢР·РҫРІР°СӮРөР»СҢ РІСӢРұСҖР°Р» С„Р°Р№Р». FullPath СҒРҫРҙРөСҖР¶РёСӮ РҝРҫР»РҪСӢР№ РҝСғСӮСҢ Рә С„Р°Р№Р»Сғ.
                string selectedFilePath = openFileDialog.FileName;

                // РһСӮРҫРұСҖР°Р¶Р°РөРј РҝСғСӮСҢ РІ РІР°СҲРөРј TextBox (РҝСҖРөРҙРҝРҫР»Р°РіР°РөСӮСҒСҸ, СҮСӮРҫ РҫРҪ РҪР°Р·СӢРІР°РөСӮСҒСҸ LocalFilePathTextBox)
                LocalFilePathTextBox.Text = selectedFilePath;
            }
        }
        private async void DownloadButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            // 1. РҹСҖРҫРІРөСҖРәРё UI
            if (IsoBox.SelectedItem is not ComboBoxItem selectedItem)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show("Р’СӢРұРөСҖРёСӮРө РҫРұСҖР°Р· РҙР»СҸ Р·Р°РіСҖСғР·РәРё РёР»Рё РәРҫРҝРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёСҸ.", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", MessageBoxButton.OK);
                return;
            }

            if (SelectedDrive == null)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show("РЎРҪР°СҮР°Р»Р° РІСӢРұРөСҖРёСӮРө USB-РҪР°РәРҫРҝРёСӮРөР»СҢ.", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", MessageBoxButton.OK);
                return;
            }

            if (!IsVentoyInstalled(SelectedDrive))
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show("РқР° РІСӢРұСҖР°РҪРҪРҫРј РҪР°РәРҫРҝРёСӮРөР»Рө РҪРө РҫРұРҪР°СҖСғР¶РөРҪ Ventoy.\nРЎРҪР°СҮР°Р»Р° СғСҒСӮР°РҪРҫРІРёСӮРө Ventoy.", "Ventoy РҪРө РҪР°Р№РҙРөРҪ", MessageBoxButton.OK);
                return;
            }

            // 2. РҹРҫРҙРіРҫСӮРҫРІРәР° РҝСғСӮРөР№
            string? tag = selectedItem.Tag?.ToString();
            string isoName = selectedItem.Content?.ToString() ?? "image.iso";

            // РӨРҫСҖРјРёСҖСғРөРј РёРјСҸ С„Р°Р№Р»Р° (Р·Р°РјРөРҪСҸРөРј РҝСҖРҫРұРөР»СӢ)
            string cleanIsoName = $"{isoName.Replace(" ", "_")}.iso";
            if (!cleanIsoName.EndsWith(".iso", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                cleanIsoName += ".iso";

            string downloads = Path.Combine(Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.UserProfile), "Downloads");
            string localTempIsoPath = Path.Combine(downloads, cleanIsoName);

            // РҹРҫР»СғСҮР°РөРј РҝСғСӮСҢ Рә РәРҫСҖРҪСҺ С„Р»РөСҲРәРё (РҪР°РҝСҖРёРјРөСҖ G:\)
            var usbDriveInfo = SelectedDrive.ToDriveInfo();
            var usbRootPath = usbDriveInfo?.RootDirectory.FullName;

            if (usbRootPath == null)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show("РқРө СғРҙР°Р»РҫСҒСҢ РҫРҝСҖРөРҙРөР»РёСӮСҢ РҝСғСӮСҢ Рә С„Р»РөСҲРәРө.", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", MessageBoxButton.OK);
                return;
            }

            // --- РқРһР’РһР•: РЎРҫР·РҙР°РөРј РҝР°РҝРәСғ ISO, РөСҒР»Рё РөС‘ РҪРөСӮ ---
            string usbIsoFolder = Path.Combine(usbRootPath, "ISO");
            if (!Directory.Exists(usbIsoFolder))
            {
                try { Directory.CreateDirectory(usbIsoFolder); }
                catch { CustomMessageBox.Show("РқРө СғРҙР°Р»РҫСҒСҢ СҒРҫР·РҙР°СӮСҢ РҝР°РҝРәСғ ISO РҪР° С„Р»РөСҲРәРө.", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", MessageBoxButton.OK); return; }
            }

            // РҳСӮРҫРіРҫРІСӢР№ РҝСғСӮСҢ РҪР° С„Р»РөСҲРәРө: G:\ISO\Windows11.iso
            string destPathOnUsb = Path.Combine(usbIsoFolder, cleanIsoName);

            try
            {
                _transferCts = new CancellationTokenSource();
                var token = _transferCts.Token;
                IsRefreshing = true;
                SetUiEnabled(false);
                UpdateProgress(0, 0);

                // --- РӣРһР“РҳРҡРҗ Р—РҗР“Р РЈР—РҡРҳ / РҡРһРҹРҳР РһР’РҗРқРҳРҜ ---
                if (IsoBox.SelectedIndex == 0) // РӣРҫРәР°Р»СҢРҪСӢР№ С„Р°Р№Р»
                {
                    string sourcePath = LocalFilePathTextBox.Text.Trim();
                    if (!File.Exists(sourcePath))
                    {
                        CustomMessageBox.Show("РЈРәР°Р¶РёСӮРө РәРҫСҖСҖРөРәСӮРҪСӢР№ РҝСғСӮСҢ Рә .ISO С„Р°Р№Р»Сғ.", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", MessageBoxButton.OK);
                        return;
                    }

                    // РҹРөСҖРөРҫРҝСҖРөРҙРөР»СҸРөРј РёРјСҸ С„Р°Р№Р»Р°, РөСҒР»Рё РәРҫРҝРёСҖСғРөРј Р»РҫРәР°Р»СҢРҪСӢР№ (СҮСӮРҫРұСӢ СҒРҫС…СҖР°РҪРёСӮСҢ РҫСҖРёРіРёРҪР°Р»СҢРҪРҫРө РёРјСҸ)
                    string localFileName = Path.GetFileName(sourcePath);
                    destPathOnUsb = Path.Combine(usbIsoFolder, localFileName);
                    cleanIsoName = localFileName; // РһРұРҪРҫРІР»СҸРөРј РёРјСҸ РҙР»СҸ JSON

                    isoText.Text = "РҡРҫРҝРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёРө ISO РІ РҝР°РҝРәСғ /ISO/ ...";
                    await Task.Run(async () => await CopyFileWithProgressAsync(sourcePath, destPathOnUsb, token), token);
                }
                else if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tag)) // РЎРәР°СҮРёРІР°РҪРёРө РёР· СҒРөСӮРё
                {
                    isoText.Text = "РҹСҖРҫРІРөСҖРәР° СҒСҒСӢР»РәРё...";
                    if (!await IsDirectDownloadLinkAsync(tag))
                    {
                        Process.Start(new ProcessStartInfo { FileName = tag, UseShellExecute = true });
                        CustomMessageBox.Show("РқРөСӮ РҝСҖСҸРјРҫР№ СҒСҒСӢР»РәРё. Р—Р°РіСҖСғР·РёСӮРө РІСҖСғСҮРҪСғСҺ.", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", MessageBoxButton.OK);
                        return;
                    }

                    await Task.Run(async () =>
                    {
                        Dispatcher.BeginInvoke(() => isoText.Text = "Р—Р°РіСҖСғР·РәР° ISO...");
                        // РЎРәР°СҮРёРІР°РөРј СҒРҪР°СҮР°Р»Р° РІ Р—Р°РіСҖСғР·РәРё
                        await DownloadFileWithProgressAsync(tag, localTempIsoPath, token);

                        token.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();

                        Dispatcher.BeginInvoke(() => isoText.Text = "РҹРөСҖРөРҪРҫСҒ РІ РҝР°РҝРәСғ /ISO/...");
                        // РҡРҫРҝРёСҖСғРөРј РёР· Р—Р°РіСҖСғР·РҫРә РҪР° РӨР»РөСҲРәСғ РІ РҝР°РҝРәСғ ISO
                        await CopyFileWithProgressAsync(localTempIsoPath, destPathOnUsb, token);
                    }, token);
                }

                // --- Р’РЁРҳР’РҗРқРҳР• OOBE (РЎ СғСҮРөСӮРҫРј РҪРҫРІРҫР№ РҝР°РҝРәРё) ---
                isoText.Text = "РқР°СҒСӮСҖРҫР№РәР° ventoy.json...";

                // РңСӢ РҝРөСҖРөРҙР°РөРј РёРјСҸ С„Р°Р№Р»Р°, СҮСӮРҫРұСӢ СҒС„РҫСҖРјРёСҖРҫРІР°СӮСҢ РҝСғСӮСҢ "/ISO/Windows.iso"
                await InjectOobeAutoAsync(usbRootPath);

                SystemSounds.Beep.Play();
                isoText.Text = "Р“РҫСӮРҫРІРҫ! РһРұСҖР°Р· РІ РҝР°РҝРәРө ISO, JSON РҫРұРҪРҫРІР»РөРҪ.";
                CustomMessageBox.Show("РһРұСҖР°Р· Р·Р°РҝРёСҒР°РҪ РІ РҝР°РҝРәСғ ISO.\nРҡРҫРҪС„РёРіСғСҖР°СҶРёСҸ Ventoy РҫРұРҪРҫРІР»РөРҪР°!", "РЈСҒРҝРөС…", MessageBoxButton.OK);
            }
            catch (OperationCanceledException)
            {
                isoText.Text = "РһРҝРөСҖР°СҶРёСҸ РҫСӮРјРөРҪРөРҪР°.";
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show($"РһСҲРёРұРәР°: {ex.Message}", "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", MessageBoxButton.OK);
                isoText.Text = "РһСҲРёРұРәР° РҫРҝРөСҖР°СҶРёРё.";
            }
            finally
            {
                IsRefreshing = false;
                SetUiEnabled(true);
                _transferCts?.Dispose();
                _transferCts = null;
                await ScanIsoImagesAsync();
            }
        }

        private void CancelButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            _transferCts?.Cancel();
            isoText.Text = "РһРҝРөСҖР°СҶРёСҸ РҫСӮРјРөРҪРөРҪР°.";
        }



        // ---------------------------
        // РҹСҖРҫРІРөСҖРәР° РҝСҖСҸРјРҫР№ СҒСҒСӢР»РәРё
        // ---------------------------
        private async Task<bool> IsDirectDownloadLinkAsync(string url)
        {
            try
            {
                using var http = new HttpClient(new HttpClientHandler
                {
                    AllowAutoRedirect = false
                });
                using var response = await http.SendAsync(new HttpRequestMessage(HttpMethod.Head, url));
                if (response.StatusCode == HttpStatusCode.Found ||
                    response.StatusCode == HttpStatusCode.MovedPermanently ||
                    response.StatusCode == HttpStatusCode.SeeOther)
                    return false; // СҖРөРҙРёСҖРөРәСӮ вҖ” РҪРө РҝСҖСҸРјР°СҸ СҒСҒСӢР»РәР°

                if (response.Content.Headers.ContentType == null)
                    return false;

                string type = response.Content.Headers.ContentType.MediaType.ToLower();
                return type.Contains("octet-stream") || type.Contains("iso");
            }
            catch
            {
                return false;
            }
        }

        // ---------------------------
        // Р—Р°РіСҖСғР·РәР° СҒ РҝСҖРҫРіСҖРөСҒСҒРҫРј
        // ---------------------------
        private async Task DownloadFileWithProgressAsync(string url, string destPath, CancellationToken token)
        {
            using var http = new HttpClient { Timeout = TimeSpan.FromHours(3) };
            using var response = await http.GetAsync(url, HttpCompletionOption.ResponseHeadersRead, token);
            response.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();

            long? totalBytes = response.Content.Headers.ContentLength;
            using var contentStream = await response.Content.ReadAsStreamAsync(token);
            using var fileStream = new FileStream(destPath, FileMode.Create, FileAccess.Write, FileShare.None, 8192, true);

            var sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();
            long totalRead = 0;
            byte[] buffer = new byte[8192];
            int bytesRead;

            _lastUpdate = DateTime.MinValue; // РЎРұСҖРҫСҒ СӮР°Р№РјРөСҖР° РҙР»СҸ РҝРөСҖРІРҫРіРҫ РҫРұРҪРҫРІР»РөРҪРёСҸ

            while ((bytesRead = await contentStream.ReadAsync(buffer, 0, buffer.Length, token)) > 0)
            {
                await fileStream.WriteAsync(buffer, 0, bytesRead, token);
                totalRead += bytesRead;

                if (totalBytes.HasValue)
                {
                    double progress = totalRead * 100.0 / totalBytes.Value;
                    double mbps = (totalRead / 1024.0 / 1024.0) / sw.Elapsed.TotalSeconds;
                    UpdateProgress(progress, mbps);
                }
            }
            UpdateProgress(100, 0);
        }

        // ---------------------------
        // РҡРҫРҝРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёРө СҒ РҝСҖРҫРіСҖРөСҒСҒРҫРј
        // ---------------------------
        private async Task CopyFileWithProgressAsync(string sourcePath, string destPath, CancellationToken token)
        {
            const int bufferSize = 1024 * 1024; // 1 MB
            long totalBytes = new FileInfo(sourcePath).Length;
            long totalRead = 0;
            var sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();

            using var source = new FileStream(sourcePath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read, FileShare.Read, bufferSize, true);
            using var dest = new FileStream(destPath, FileMode.Create, FileAccess.Write, FileShare.None, bufferSize, true);

            byte[] buffer = new byte[bufferSize];
            int bytesRead;
            _lastUpdate = DateTime.MinValue; // РЎРұСҖРҫСҒ СӮР°Р№РјРөСҖР° РҙР»СҸ РҝРөСҖРІРҫРіРҫ РҫРұРҪРҫРІР»РөРҪРёСҸ

            while ((bytesRead = await source.ReadAsync(buffer, 0, buffer.Length, token)) > 0)
            {
                await dest.WriteAsync(buffer, 0, bytesRead, token);
                totalRead += bytesRead;

                double progress = totalRead * 100.0 / totalBytes;
                double mbps = (totalRead / 1024.0 / 1024.0) / sw.Elapsed.TotalSeconds;
                UpdateProgress(progress, mbps);
            }
            UpdateProgress(100, 0);
        }

        // ---------------------------
        // РһРұРҪРҫРІР»РөРҪРёРө РҝСҖРҫРіСҖРөСҒСҒР° (РІ isoText)
        // ---------------------------
        private void UpdateProgress(double percent, double mbps)
        {
            // РһРіСҖР°РҪРёСҮРёРІР°РөРј СҮР°СҒСӮРҫСӮСғ РҫРұРҪРҫРІР»РөРҪРёСҸ UI (РҪРө СҮР°СүРө 6вҖ“7 СҖР°Р· РІ СҒРөРәСғРҪРҙСғ)
            if ((DateTime.Now - _lastUpdate).TotalMilliseconds < MinUpdateIntervalMs && percent < 100)
                return;

            _lastUpdate = DateTime.Now;

            // РҳСҒРҝРҫР»СҢР·СғРөРј BeginInvoke вҖ” РқР• Р¶РҙС‘Рј РІСӢРҝРҫР»РҪРөРҪРёСҸ, РҝСҖРҫСҒСӮРҫ РұСҖРҫСҒР°РөРј РІ РҫСҮРөСҖРөРҙСҢ UI
            Dispatcher.BeginInvoke(() =>
            {
                if (progressBar != null)
                    progressBar.Value = percent;

                if (isoText != null)
                    isoText.Text = percent >= 100
                        ? "Р—Р°РІРөСҖСҲРөРҪРҫ"
                        : $"{percent:F1}% ({mbps:F2} РңР‘/СҒ)";
            }, DispatcherPriority.Background); // РёР»Рё Render
        }
        private void SetUiEnabled(bool enabled)
        {
            // РІСҒС‘, РәСҖРҫРјРө РәРҪРҫРҝРәРё "РһСӮРјРөРҪР°"
            IsoBox.IsEnabled = enabled;
            DownloadButton.IsEnabled = enabled;
            Browse.IsEnabled = enabled;
            if (IsoBox.SelectedIndex == 0)
            {
                LocalFilePathTextBox.IsEnabled = enabled;
            }
            DrivesListView.IsEnabled = enabled;
            RefreshButton.IsEnabled = enabled;
            UpdateButton.IsEnabled = enabled;
            InstallButton.IsEnabled = enabled;

            CancelButton.IsEnabled = !enabled; // РҪР°РҫРұРҫСҖРҫСӮ: РөСҒР»Рё РёРҪСӮРөСҖС„РөР№СҒ РІСӢРәР»СҺСҮРөРҪ вҖ” РҫСӮРјРөРҪР° РІРәР»СҺСҮРөРҪР°
        }
        private bool IsVentoyInstalled(UsbDriveItem usbRoot)
        {
            try
            {
                if (usbRoot.DisplayName.ToLower().Contains("ventoy") && !usbRoot.DisplayName.ToLower().Contains("efi"))
                    return true;
                else
                {
                    CustomMessageBox.Show("Р’РөСҖРҫСҸСӮРҪРҫ, Ventoy РҪРө СғСҒСӮР°РҪРҫРІР»РөРҪ РҪР° РҪР°РәРҫРҝРёСӮРөР»Рө, РёР»Рё РІСӢ РҝСӢСӮР°РөСӮРөСҒСҢ РІР·Р°РёРјРҫРҙРөР№СҒСӮРІРҫРІР°СӮСҢ СҒ EFI СҖР°Р·РҙРөР»РҫРј Ventoy","");
                    return false;
                }
                    
            }
            catch
            {
                return false;
            }
        }
        private async void Button_Click_1(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (ImagesList.SelectedItem != null)
            {
                var resp = CustomMessageBox.Show("Р’СӢ СӮРҫСҮРҪРҫ С…РҫСӮРёСӮРө СғРҙР°Р»РёСӮСҢ РҫРұСҖР°Р· СҒ РІСӢРұСҖР°РҪРҪРҫРіРҫ РҪР°РәРҫРҝРёСӮРөР»СҸ?", "", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.YesNo);
                if (resp == CustomMessageBox.MessageBoxResult.Yes)
                {
                    string path = (ImagesList.SelectedItem as IsoImageItem).FullPath;
                    File.Delete(path);
                    await ScanIsoImagesAsync();
                }
            }
            else { CustomMessageBox.Show("РЎРҪР°СҮР°Р»Р° РІСӢРұРөСҖРёСӮРө С„Р°Р№Р» РҙР»СҸ СғРҙР°Р»РөРҪРёСҸ", "", System.Windows.MessageBoxButton.OK); }
            
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// РҡРҫРҝРёСҖСғРөСӮ autounattend.xml РёР· Р»РҫРәР°Р»СҢРҪРҫР№ РҝР°РҝРәРё Assets РІ РәРҫСҖРөРҪСҢ С„Р»РөСҲРәРё.
        /// </summary>
        private async Task CreateAutounattend(string driveRootPath)
        {
            try
            {
                // 1. Р’СӢСҮРёСҒР»СҸРөРј РҝСғСӮСҢ Рә РёСҒС…РҫРҙРҪРҫРјСғ С„Р°Р№Р»Сғ.
                // AppDomain.CurrentDomain.BaseDirectory вҖ” СҚСӮРҫ РҝР°РҝРәР°, РіРҙРө Р»РөР¶РёСӮ Р·Р°РҝСғСүРөРҪРҪСӢР№ .exe
                string sourcePath = Path.Combine(AppDomain.CurrentDomain.BaseDirectory, "Assets", "autounattend.xml");

                // 2. Р’СӢСҮРёСҒР»СҸРөРј РҝСғСӮСҢ РҪР°Р·РҪР°СҮРөРҪРёСҸ (РәРҫСҖРөРҪСҢ С„Р»РөСҲРәРё)
                string destPath = Path.Combine(driveRootPath, "autounattend.xml");

                // 3. РҹСҖРҫРІРөСҖСҸРөРј, СҒСғСүРөСҒСӮРІСғРөСӮ Р»Рё С„Р°Р№Р» РІ РҝР°РҝРәРө РҝСҖРҫРіСҖР°РјРјСӢ
                if (!File.Exists(sourcePath))
                {
                    CustomMessageBox.Show($"РӨР°Р№Р» РҪРө РҪР°Р№РҙРөРҪ РҝРҫ РҝСғСӮРё:\n{sourcePath}\n\nРЈРұРөРҙРёСӮРөСҒСҢ, СҮСӮРҫ РҝР°РҝРәР° 'Assets' СҒСғСүРөСҒСӮРІСғРөСӮ СҖСҸРҙРҫРј СҒ exe Рё РІ РҪРөР№ РөСҒСӮСҢ С„Р°Р№Р».",
                                    "РһСҲРёРұРәР° РәРҫРҪС„РёРіСғСҖР°СҶРёРё", MessageBoxButton.OK);
                    return;
                }

                // 4. РҡРҫРҝРёСҖСғРөРј С„Р°Р№Р» (overwrite: true СҖР°Р·СҖРөСҲР°РөСӮ Р·Р°РјРөРҪСғ СҒСӮР°СҖРҫРіРҫ С„Р°Р№Р»Р°)
                // РҳСҒРҝРҫР»СҢР·СғРөРј Task.Run, СҮСӮРҫРұСӢ РҫРҝРөСҖР°СҶРёСҸ РІРІРҫРҙР°-РІСӢРІРҫРҙР° РҪРө РјРҫСҖРҫР·РёР»Р° РёРҪСӮРөСҖС„РөР№СҒ
                await Task.Run(() =>
                {
                    File.Copy(sourcePath, destPath, true);
                });

                // (РһРҝСҶРёРҫРҪР°Р»СҢРҪРҫ) РңРҫР¶РҪРҫ РІСӢРІРөСҒСӮРё СҒРҫРҫРұСүРөРҪРёРө РҫРұ СғСҒРҝРөС…Рө РёР»Рё РҝСҖРҫСҒСӮРҫ РјРҫР»СҮР° РҝСҖРҫРҙРҫР»Р¶РёСӮСҢ
                // MessageBox.Show("РӨР°Р№Р» РҫСӮРІРөСӮРҫРІ СғСҒРҝРөСҲРҪРҫ СҒРәРҫРҝРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪ!", "РЈСҒРҝРөС…", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Information);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show($"РһСҲРёРұРәР° РҝСҖРё РәРҫРҝРёСҖРҫРІР°РҪРёРё autounattend.xml: {ex.Message}",
                                "РһСҲРёРұРәР°", MessageBoxButton.OK);
            }
        }

        private async Task InjectOobeAutoAsync(string usbRootPath)
        {
            string ventoyDir = Path.Combine(usbRootPath, "ventoy");
            string jsonPath = Path.Combine(ventoyDir, "ventoy.json");
            if (!Path.Exists(ventoyDir))
            {
                Directory.CreateDirectory(ventoyDir);
            }
            try
            {
                IsRefreshing = true;

                // РқР°СҒСӮСҖРҫР№РәР° JSON (РҹСҖР°РІРёР»СҢРҪР°СҸ РІРөСҖСҒРёСҸ СҒ РҝРҫР»РҪРҫР№ РҝРөСҖРөР·Р°РҝРёСҒСҢСҺ)
                Dispatcher.Invoke(() => isoText.Text = "РқР°СҒСӮСҖРҫР№РәР° Ventoy (JSON)...");

                var ventoyConfig = new
                {
                    control = new[]
    {
        new { VTOY_MENU_LANGUAGE = "ru_RU" }
    },
                    auto_install = new[]
    {
        new
        {
            parent = "/ISO",      // РҹР°РҝРәР°, Рә РҫРұСҖР°Р·Р°Рј РІ РәРҫСӮРҫСҖРҫР№ РҝСҖРёРјРөРҪРёСӮСҒСҸ СҒРәСҖРёРҝСӮ
            template = new[]
            {
                "/autounattend.xml" // РҹСғСӮСҢ Рә СҒРәСҖРёРҝСӮСғ (РІ РәРҫСҖРҪРө С„Р»РөСҲРәРё)
            }
        }
    }
                };

                var jsonOptions = new JsonSerializerOptions { WriteIndented = true };
                string jsonString = JsonSerializer.Serialize(ventoyConfig, jsonOptions);
                File.WriteAllText(jsonPath, jsonString, Encoding.UTF8);
                await CreateAutounattend(usbRootPath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                CustomMessageBox.Show(ex.Message,"");
            }
            finally
            {
                IsRefreshing = false;
            }
        }

        private async void InjectOnlyButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var root = SelectedDrive.ToDriveInfo()?.RootDirectory.FullName;
            if (root == null || !IsVentoyInstalled(SelectedDrive)) return;
            await InjectOobeAutoAsync(root);
            isoText.Text = "Р“РҫСӮРҫРІРҫ!";
        }
    }



    public class UsbDriveItem : INotifyPropertyChanged
    {
        public event PropertyChangedEventHandler? PropertyChanged;

        public string DriveLetter { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string VolumeLabel { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string DisplayName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        private long _totalBytes;
        public long TotalBytes { get => _totalBytes; set { _totalBytes = value; OnProp(nameof(TotalBytes)); } }

        private long _freeBytes;
        public long FreeBytes { get => _freeBytes; set { _freeBytes = value; OnProp(nameof(FreeBytes)); } }

        private double _usedPercent;
        public double UsedPercent { get => _usedPercent; set { _usedPercent = value; OnProp(nameof(UsedPercent)); } }

        private void OnProp(string n) => PropertyChanged?.Invoke(this, new PropertyChangedEventArgs(n));

        public DriveInfo? ToDriveInfo()
        {
            try
            {
                var letter = DriveLetter;
                if (!letter.EndsWith(":"))
                    letter = letter.Length == 1 ? letter + ":" : letter.TrimEnd('\\');
                return new DriveInfo(letter);
            }
            catch { return null; }
        }
    }
    public class IsoItem
    {
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? DownloadUrl { get; set; } // null РҙР»СҸ Р»РҫРәР°Р»СҢРҪРҫРіРҫ С„Р°Р№Р»Р°
    }

}

=== FILE: D:\Visual Studio Projects\Helinstaller\Views\Windows\ActivationDialog.xaml.cs ===
using System;
using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Text.RegularExpressions;
using System.Windows;
using System.Windows.Media;
using Wpf.Ui.Controls;

namespace Helinstaller.Views.Pages
{
    public partial class ActivationDialog : FluentWindow
    {
        private Process _psProcess;
        private readonly string _scriptUrl = "https://get.activated.win";
        private bool _isSuccessDetected = false;

        public ActivationDialog()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
            Closing += (s, e) => { try { _psProcess?.Kill(); } catch { } };
        }

        private void ActivationBtn_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (sender is not Wpf.Ui.Controls.Button btn || btn.Tag == null) return;

            string switchArg = btn.Tag.ToString();

            // РЎРұСҖРҫСҒ СҒРҫСҒСӮРҫСҸРҪРёСҸ РҝРөСҖРөРҙ Р·Р°РҝСғСҒРәРҫРј
            _isSuccessDetected = false;
            ButtonsContainer.IsEnabled = false;
            LoadingRing.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;
            DebugLog.Text = $"--- Р—Р°РҝСғСҒРә: {btn.Content} ({switchArg}) ---\n";
            StatusText.Foreground = (Brush)FindResource("TextFillColorPrimaryBrush");
            StatusText.Text = "РҹРҫРҙРәР»СҺСҮРөРҪРёРө Рә СҒРөСҖРІРөСҖСғ...";
            SubtitleText.Text = "Р’СӢРҝРҫР»РҪСҸРөСӮСҒСҸ СҒРәСҖРёРҝСӮ... РҹРҫР¶Р°Р»СғР№СҒСӮР°, РҝРҫРҙРҫР¶РҙРёСӮРө.";

            RunActivationScript(switchArg);
        }

        private void RunActivationScript(string argument)
        {
            _psProcess = new Process();
            _psProcess.StartInfo = new ProcessStartInfo
            {
                FileName = "powershell.exe",
                Arguments = $"-NoProfile -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -Command \"[Net.ServicePointManager]::SecurityProtocol = [Net.SecurityProtocolType]::Tls12; $s = Invoke-RestMethod -Uri '{_scriptUrl}'; $s = [scriptblock]::Create($s); & $s {argument}\"",
                UseShellExecute = false,
                RedirectStandardOutput = true,
                RedirectStandardError = true,
                CreateNoWindow = true,
                StandardOutputEncoding = System.Text.Encoding.UTF8
            };

            _psProcess.OutputDataReceived += (s, e) => {
                if (e.Data != null) Dispatcher.Invoke(() => {
                    string cleanLine = Regex.Replace(e.Data, @"\x1B\[[^@-~]*[@-~]", "").Trim();

                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(cleanLine))
                    {
                        DebugLog.Text += cleanLine + Environment.NewLine;
                        DebugLog.ScrollToEnd();
                        StatusText.Text = cleanLine;

                        // РҳРқРўР•РӣРӣР•РҡРўРЈРҗРӣР¬РқР«Рҷ РҹРҗР РЎРҳРқР“ РЈРЎРҹР•РҘРҗ
                        // MAS РҫРұСӢСҮРҪРҫ РҝРёСҲРөСӮ "Product activated successfully" РёР»Рё "Permanently Activated"
                        if (cleanLine.Contains("successfully", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                            cleanLine.Contains("Activated", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                            cleanLine.Contains("Success", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                        {
                            _isSuccessDetected = true;
                        }
                    }
                });
            };

            _psProcess.ErrorDataReceived += (s, e) => {
                if (e.Data != null) Dispatcher.Invoke(() => {
                    DebugLog.Text += "РһРЁРҳР‘РҡРҗ: " + e.Data + Environment.NewLine;
                });
            };

            _psProcess.EnableRaisingEvents = true;
            _psProcess.Exited += (s, e) => Dispatcher.Invoke(() => {
                ButtonsContainer.IsEnabled = true;
                LoadingRing.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;

                var msg = new Wpf.Ui.Controls.MessageBox();
                msg.Title = "Р РөР·СғР»СҢСӮР°СӮ Р°РәСӮРёРІР°СҶРёРё";

                if (_isSuccessDetected)
                {
                    StatusText.Text = "РҗРәСӮРёРІР°СҶРёСҸ Р·Р°РІРөСҖСҲРөРҪР° СғСҒРҝРөСҲРҪРҫ!";
                    StatusText.Foreground = Brushes.LightGreen;
                    SubtitleText.Text = "РЎРёСҒСӮРөРјР° РіРҫСӮРҫРІР° Рә РёСҒРҝРҫР»СҢР·РҫРІР°РҪРёСҺ.";
                    msg.Content = "РҹСҖРҫСҶРөСҒСҒ Р·Р°РІРөСҖСҲРөРҪ СғСҒРҝРөСҲРҪРҫ! РӣРёСҶРөРҪР·РёСҸ СғСҒСӮР°РҪРҫРІР»РөРҪР°.";
                }
                else
                {
                    StatusText.Text = "РҹСҖРҫСҶРөСҒСҒ Р·Р°РІРөСҖСҲРөРҪ.";
                    StatusText.Foreground = Brushes.Orange;
                    SubtitleText.Text = "РҹСҖРҫРІРөСҖСҢСӮРө СҒСӮР°СӮСғСҒ РІ РҪР°СҒСӮСҖРҫР№РәР°С… Windows.";
                    msg.Content = "РЎРәСҖРёРҝСӮ Р·Р°РІРөСҖСҲРёР» СҖР°РұРҫСӮСғ. Р•СҒР»Рё Р°РәСӮРёРІР°СҶРёСҸ РҪРө РҝСҖРҫСҲР»Р°, РҝСҖРҫРІРөСҖСҢСӮРө Р»РҫРі РҪР° РҪР°Р»РёСҮРёРө РҫСҲРёРұРҫРә.";
                }

                msg.ShowDialogAsync();
            });

            try
            {
                _psProcess.Start();
                _psProcess.BeginOutputReadLine();
                _psProcess.BeginErrorReadLine();
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                var msg = new Wpf.Ui.Controls.MessageBox();
                msg.Content = "РһСҲРёРұРәР° Р·Р°РҝСғСҒРәР°: " + ex.Message;
                msg.ShowDialogAsync();
                ButtonsContainer.IsEnabled = true;
                LoadingRing.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
            }
        }

        private void Button_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            this.Close();
        }
    }
}

using System.Windows.Controls;
using Wpf.Ui.Controls;
using MessageBoxButton = System.Windows.MessageBoxButton;
namespace Helinstaller
{
    public partial class CustomMessageBox : FluentWindow
    {
        public enum MessageBoxResult
        {
            OK,
            Cancel,
            Yes,
            No,
            None
        }

        public MessageBoxResult Result { get; private set; } = MessageBoxResult.None;

        public CustomMessageBox(string message, string title, MessageBoxButton buttons)
        {
            InitializeComponent();
            Title = title;
            MessageText.Text = message;
            CreateButtons(buttons);
        }

        private void CreateButtons(MessageBoxButton buttons)
        {
            if (buttons == MessageBoxButton.OK || buttons == MessageBoxButton.OKCancel)
            {
                var okButton = new Wpf.Ui.Controls.Button { Content = "РһРҡ", Margin = new Thickness(5, 0, 0, 0), Appearance = ControlAppearance.Secondary };
                okButton.Click += (sender, e) => { Result = MessageBoxResult.OK; Close(); };
                (FindName("ButtonPanel") as StackPanel)?.Children.Add(okButton);
            }
            if (buttons == MessageBoxButton.OKCancel)
            {
                var cancelButton = new Wpf.Ui.Controls.Button { Content = "РһСӮРјРөРҪР°", Margin = new Thickness(5, 0, 0, 0), Appearance = ControlAppearance.Secondary };
                cancelButton.Click += (sender, e) => { Result = MessageBoxResult.Cancel; Close(); };
                (FindName("ButtonPanel") as StackPanel)?.Children.Add(cancelButton);
            }
            if (buttons == MessageBoxButton.YesNo || buttons == MessageBoxButton.YesNoCancel)
            {
                var yesButton = new Wpf.Ui.Controls.Button { Content = "Р”Р°", Margin = new Thickness(5, 0, 0, 0), Appearance = ControlAppearance.Secondary };
                yesButton.Click += (sender, e) => { Result = MessageBoxResult.Yes; Close(); };
                (FindName("ButtonPanel") as StackPanel)?.Children.Add(yesButton);

                var noButton = new Wpf.Ui.Controls.Button { Content = "РқРөСӮ", Margin = new Thickness(5, 0, 0, 0), Appearance = ControlAppearance.Secondary };
                noButton.Click += (sender, e) => { Result = MessageBoxResult.No; Close(); };
                (FindName("ButtonPanel") as StackPanel)?.Children.Add(noButton);
            }
            if (buttons == MessageBoxButton.YesNoCancel)
            {
                var cancelButton = new Wpf.Ui.Controls.Button { Content = "РһСӮРјРөРҪР°", Margin = new Thickness(5, 0, 0, 0), Appearance = ControlAppearance.Secondary };
                cancelButton.Click += (sender, e) => { Result = MessageBoxResult.Cancel; Close(); };
                (FindName("ButtonPanel") as StackPanel)?.Children.Add(cancelButton);
            }
        }

        public static MessageBoxResult Show(string message, string title = "РЎРҫРҫРұСүРөРҪРёРө", MessageBoxButton buttons = MessageBoxButton.OK)
        {
            var dialog = new CustomMessageBox(message, title, buttons);
            dialog.ShowDialog();
            return dialog.Result;
        }
    }
}

using CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.Messaging;
